      - Use the *drop* (or *put down*) action to put the pepper onto the tabletop.

      - If you opened a fridge/cabinet, close it after retrieving the pepper to keep the environment tidy.

3. **Verify completion**  
   - Perform a quick *look* or *inspect* of the table to confirm that every pepper is now on it.  
   - If any pepper is missing, return to step 2 for that pepper.

4. **Finish**  
   - Stop actions once all peppers are confirmed on the table. No extra movements or interactions are needed.
